To the mixture of labeled reference and sample RNA, 20 g human COT-1 DNA (Invitrogen, Carlsbad, CA), 8 g yeast tRNA (Invitrogen) and 20 g polyadenylic acid (Sigma-Aldrich, St. Louis, MO) were added.///taxid_ch2: 9606///hyb_protocol: Preheated hybridization buffer (25% formamide, 5 SSC, 0.1% SDS) was added and arrays were hybridised overnight 42C to human 35K oligo microarrays///scan_protocol: Scanned on an Agilent G2565BA scanner.///description: Expanded descriptions of Channel 1 'Characteristics':///description.1: TEM: transanal endoscopic microsurgical resection. The Limma (linear models for microarray data) package of Bioconductor (http://www.bioconductor.org) was used for importing the data, normalizing the arrays and identifying differentially expressed genes. To the mixture of labeled reference and sample RNA, 20 g human COT-1 DNA (Invitrogen, Carlsbad, CA), 8 g yeast tRNA (Invitrogen) and 20 g polyadenylic acid (Sigma-Aldrich, St. Louis, MO) were added.///taxid_ch2: 9606///hyb_protocol: Preheated hybridization buffer (25% formamide, 5 SSC, 0.1% SDS) was added and arrays were hybridised overnight 42C to human 35K oligo microarrays///scan_protocol: Scanned on an Agilent G2565BA scanner.///description: Expanded descriptions of Channel 1 'Characteristics':///description.1: TEM: transanal endoscopic microsurgical resection. The Limma (linear models for microarray data) package of Bioconductor (http://www.bioconductor.org) was used for importing the data, normalizing the arrays and identifying differentially expressed genes. Control spots and spots with more than 10% saturation, a diameter smaller than 60 m or signal intensity less than 20 counts above background were excluded from the analysis. To the mixture of labeled reference and sample RNA, 20 g human COT-1 DNA (Invitrogen, Carlsbad, CA), 8 g yeast tRNA (Invitrogen) and 20 g polyadenylic acid (Sigma-Aldrich, St. Louis, MO) were added.///taxid_ch2: 9606///hyb_protocol: Preheated hybridization buffer (25% formamide, 5 SSC, 0.1% SDS) was added and arrays were hybridised overnight 42C to human 35K oligo microarrays///scan_protocol: Scanned on an Agilent G2565BA scanner.///description: Expanded descriptions of Channel 1 'Characteristics':///description.1: TEM: transanal endoscopic microsurgical resection. The Limma (linear models for microarray data) package of Bioconductor (http://www.bioconductor.org) was used for importing the data, normalizing the arrays and identifying differentially expressed genes. Data were corrected for local background (method normexp) and normalized within arrays by print-tip loess normalization and between arrays by quantile normalization.///platform_id: GPL3676///contact_name: Esther,,Lips///contact_email: e.lips@nki.nl///contact_phone: +31-20-5122039///contact_fax: +31-20-5122050///contact_department: Experimental Therapy///contact_institute: NKI-AVL///contact_address: Plesmanlaan 121///contact_city: Amsterdam///contact_zip.postal_code: 1066 CX ///contact_country: Netherlands///supplementary_file: ftp://ftp.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pub/geo/DATA/supplementary/samples/GSM307nnn/GSM307345/GSM307345.gpr.gz///supplementary_file.1: ///supplementary_file.2: ///data_row_count: 33091"

Data were corrected for local background (method normexp) and normalized within arrays by print-tip loess normalization and between arrays by quantile normalization.///platform_id: GPL3676///contact_name: Esther,,Lips///contact_email: e.lips@nki.nl///contact_phone: +31-20-5122039///contact_fax: +31-20-5122050///contact_department: Experimental Therapy///contact_institute: NKI-AVL///contact_address: Plesmanlaan 121///contact_city: Amsterdam///contact_zip.postal_code: 1066 CX ///contact_country: Netherlands///supplementary_file: ftp://ftp.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pub/geo/DATA/supplementary/samples/GSM307nnn/GSM307371/GSM307371.gpr.gz///supplementary_file.1: ///supplementary_file.2: ///data_row_count: 33091"
